Installation\n     </h1>\n     <p>\n      You can install this plugin with either\n      <a href="http://bower.io/" target="_blank">\n       Bower\n      </a>\n      or\n      <a href="https://www.npmjs.org/" target="_blank">\n       NPM\n      </a>\n      :\n     </p>\n     <prism source="app/samples/bower-npm-install">\n      <pre class="language-markup"><code>bower install angular-form-for --save\n  npm install angular-form-for --save\n</code></pre>\n     </prism>\n     <p>\n      This will create an\n      <code>\n       angular-form-for\n      </code>\n      folder within your\n      <code>\n       bower_components\n      </code>\n      or\n      <code>\n       node_components\n      </code>\n      directory.\n    Inside of that folder there will be a\n      <code>\n       dist\n      </code>\n      folder with the formFor JavaScript and CSS files.\n     </p>\n     <p>\n      Next include the formFor module in your Angular application like so:\n     </p>\n     <prism parser="javascript" source="app/samples/module-definition.js">\n      <pre class="language-javascript"><code><span class="token comment" spellcheck="true">// formFor directives and services only; no templates\n</span>angular<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">module<span class="token punctuation">(</span></span><span class="token string">\'myAngularApp\'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">\'formFor\'</span><span class="token templates\n</span>angular<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">module<span class="token punctuation">(</span></span><span class="token string">\'myAngularApp\'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">\'formFor\'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">\'formFor.bootstrapTemplates\'</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>\n\n<span class="token comment" spellcheck="true">// formFor and Angular "Material Design" templates\n</span>angular<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">module<span class="token punctuation">(</span></span><span class="token string">\'myAngularApp\'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token
